    So instead of each tool being its own silo, you're building one unified 
   agentic layer                                                            
     where:                                                                 
                                                                            
    - AG-UI is the protocol backbone вҖ” streaming events, shared state,      
  human-in-the-loop                                                         
    interrupts between your agent(s) and whatever frontend you build        
    - Your comms client and content client (ClipBot) become MCP tool        
  servers that any                                                          
    agent can call                                                          
    - The Lemon-style voice/overlay UX becomes the universal entry point вҖ”  
  you talk, the                                                             
    agent orchestrates across your tools via AG-UI events                   
                                                                            
    The killer part is the AG-UI spec already accounts for the hard         
  problems: nested                                                          
    agent delegation (your comms agent can call your content agent),        
  streaming                                                                 
    intermediate results back to the UI, and human-in-the-loop for approval 
   flows вҖ” which                                                            
     for comms (sending messages) and content (publishing) you absolutely   
  want.                                                                     
                                                                            
    What makes this crazy-good vs just crazy                                
                                                                            
    The AG-UI architecture diagram literally breaks it into three protocol  
  layers:                                                                   
    - AG-UI = Agent вҶ” User (your overlay/voice interface)                   
    - MCP = Agent вҶ” Tools (your Claude connectors, comms client, content    
  client)                                                                   
    - A2A = Agent вҶ” Agent (your comms client talking to your content        
  client)                                                                   
                                                                            
    You're not inventing a new protocol вҖ” you're wiring your existing tools 
   into an open                                                             
    standard that already has SDK support (JS, Go, Rust, etc.) and          
  framework integrations                                                    
     (LangGraph, Mastra, etc.).                                             
                                                                            
    The real question                                                       
                                                                            
    Where do you want to start pulling this together? Are you thinking:     
                                                                            
    1. AG-UI as the protocol layer first вҖ” standardize how your existing    
  clients expose                                                            
    themselves, then build the unified frontend on top                      
    2. Voice/overlay UX first вҖ” build the Lemon-style interaction layer and 
   wire it to                                                               
    your existing tools                                                     
    3. Agent orchestration first вҖ” get comms + content client talking to    
  each other via                                                            
    A2A, then wrap it in AG-UI                                              
                                                                            
    What's the state of the comms client and ClipBot right now? I want to   
  understand how                                                            
    far along the pieces are so we can figure out where the AG-UI protocol  
  layer plugs in                                                            
     most naturally.

    в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  ---
  Why This Is Crazy-Good (Not Just Crazy)

  AG-UI already solves the hard problems you'd otherwise build custom:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ      Problem      в”Ӯ Your current approach в”Ӯ       AG-UI gives you        в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ Streaming tool    в”Ӯ Custom SSE (ClipBot's в”Ӯ Built-in event streaming     в”Ӯ

  The AG-UI protocol is literally the layer between your agents and your UI. And
   it already has SDK support in JS, Go, Rust, plus framework integrations with
  LangGraph, Mastra, CrewAI, and more.

  ---
  The Practical Question: What Do You Build Next?

  Here's my honest take:

                          DON'T DO THIS:
                          вқҢ Stop everything and build AG-UI layer now
                          (you have no tools to connect to yet)


                          DO THIS INSTEAD:

  Phase 1 (NOW):          Build the TOOLS, not the UI
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Terminal 1:         Comms Client tools    вҶҗ already building
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Terminal 2:         ClipBot MCP server    вҶҗ exists, needs MCP exposed
  в””в”Җв”Җ Terminal 3:         Research tools        вҶҗ next up

  Phase 2 (NEXT WEEK):   Wire AG-UI as the unified protocol
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Each client becomes an MCP server (no UI needed)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ One AG-UI frontend replaces all three UIs
  в””в”Җв”Җ Voice layer (Lemon-style) on top

  Phase 3 (AFTER):       A2A between agents
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Comms agent calls Research agent automatically
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ Content agent calls Comms agent to distribute
  в””в”Җв”Җ Full autonomous pipeline

  The key insight: if AG-UI is your endgame, the Research Client doesn't need 
  its own UI. It just needs to be an MCP tool server. Same for Comms. Same for
  ClipBot. The UIs you're building now are stepping stones вҖ” the real interface
  is the unified AG-UI layer.

  ---
  So What Should the Research Client Look Like?

  Don't build a UI. Build it as a headless tool server from day one:

  research/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ src/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ tools/                    # The actual capabilities
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ deep-research.ts      # Perplexity API wrapper
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ scrape.ts             # Firecrawl / Playwright
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ browse.ts             # Playwright MCP
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ find-opportunities.ts # Reddit + search trends
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ generate-brief.ts     # AI compiles research вҶ’ doc
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ mcp/
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ server.ts             # Exposes tools as MCP server
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ types/
  в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ brief.ts              # Brief, Source, Finding
  в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ config.ts
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ package.json
  в””в”Җв”Җ research.config.json

  No Next.js. No UI. No sidebar. Just tools + MCP server.

  Why? Because the AG-UI unified frontend IS the UI. The Research Client's job
  is to answer when called, not to have its own window. You'd talk to it through
   the unified voice/chat interface:

  You: "Research cannabis tech market in Colorado"
    вҶ’ Orchestrator routes to Research MCP
      вҶ’ deep-research tool calls Perplexity
      вҶ’ scrape tool crawls competitor sites
      вҶ’ generate-brief compiles findings
      вҶ’ AG-UI streams results back to your chat
      вҶ’ You: "Now find 50 leads from that research"
        вҶ’ Orchestrator routes to Comms MCP
          вҶ’ search_contacts with the research context

  ---
  The Build Order (Revised With AG-UI Endgame)

  THIS WEEKEND:
    Terminal 1: Comms Client (building now вҖ” keep going)
    Terminal 2: Research tools (headless, MCP server only)

  NEXT WEEK:
    Terminal 3: ClipBot MCP server (expose existing tools)
    Terminal 4: AG-UI prototype (one chat interface вҶ’ all three MCPs)

  AFTER:
    Voice layer (Lemon-style overlay)
    A2A agent delegation
    Kill the individual client UIs

  This is the right order because you need the hands (tools) before you need the
   nervous system (AG-UI) before you need the voice (Lemon). But knowing AG-UI
  is the endgame means you build the Research Client as a headless MCP server
  from the start вҖ” no throwaway UI work.

  What do you think? Does this match the vision in your head?

  в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  No pages. No routes. No sidebar. The UI is the output of the agent. The agent
  reads context from your MCP clients (what emails are pending, what clips are
  processing, what automations are running) and renders the right interface on
  the fly.

  AG-UI's spec literally has this built in:

  Two types of generative UI in AG-UI:

  1. Static Generative UI
     вҶ’ Agent outputs typed components
     вҶ’ "Here's an ApprovalCard, here's a ContactList, here's a VideoTimeline"
     вҶ’ Renders as real interactive React components

  2. Declarative Generative UI
     вҶ’ Agent uses a small declarative language
     вҶ’ "Show a table of contacts with columns: name, email, score, last contact"
     вҶ’ UI renderer interprets and builds it

  This means your clients don't need UIs at all. They need:

  What each client ACTUALLY needs:

    ClipBot     вҶ’ tools + MCP server     (already has tools, needs MCP)
    Comms       вҶ’ tools + MCP server     (building now)
    Research    вҶ’ tools + MCP server     (next)

  What you build ONCE:

    The Shell   вҶ’ agent bar + generative UI renderer + AG-UI client
                 вҶ’ this is the only "app" the user ever opens
                 вҶ’ voice in, dynamic UI out

  Go learn AG-UI. This changes the whole game вҖ” the Comms Client building right
  now is still right (you need the tools), but the UI it's building is temporary
   scaffolding. The real UI is the generative one that sits on top of
  everything.

  Save this idea somewhere before it gets lost in terminal history.

    Comms Client - Built

    What was built:

    - Commander.js CLI with init, config, ui, cron commands

    toUIMessageStreamResponse(), stopWhen: stepCountIs(10)

  approvals

    cd comms/ui && npm run dev                 # UI on localhost:3000

  Now вҖ” you said you wanted to move to Research. Given the AG-UI conversation,
  do you want to:

  1. Build Research as a headless MCP tool server (no UI, just tools вҖ” the AG-UI
   endgame approach)

  Based on everything we discussed, I'd say go headless. The Research Client is
  the first one you can build "right" from the start вҖ” tools only, MCP server,
  no throwaway UI. It becomes the proof of concept for the AG-UI architecture
  where the UI generates itself.

в—Ҹ OK. Here's the stack doc list vs reality:

  STACK DOC SAYS:                    ROOT-LEVEL ANALYSIS:

  Perplexity API                     вң… KEEP вҖ” $20/mo Pro, no self-hosted
  alternative
                                        Best AI research engine. Has MCP server.

  NotebookLM                         вқҢ CUT вҖ” it's a Google product you use
  manually
                                        Can't API into it. Not a tool you wire
  up.

  IdeaBrowser                        рҹ”¶ MAYBE вҖ” niche. Reddit + trends.
                                        Could DIY with Reddit API + Google
  Trends API

  Firecrawl                          вң… KEEP вҖ” web scraping as a service. Has
  MCP.
                                        Free tier: 500 credits/mo
                                        OR self-host (it's open source)

  Playwright MCP                     вң… KEEP вҖ” free, open source, has official
  MCP
                                        Browser automation. Zero cost.

  ClawdCursor                        вқҢ CUT вҖ” desktop automation is a
  distraction
                                        Research client doesn't need to click
  GUIs

  OpenClaw                           вқҢ CUT вҖ” VM-based computer use agent
                                        Cool but overkill for research

  Orgo                               вқҢ CUT вҖ” spin up VMs? For research?
                                        Way over-engineered

  Half that list is noise. The Research Client needs 3 core capabilities:

  1. SEARCH    вҖ” find information on any topic
  2. SCRAPE    вҖ” extract data from websites
  3. SYNTHESIZE вҖ” compile findings into briefs

  The core value: ask research questions in natural language, get structured
  briefs
  back with sources. Scrape competitor sites, search Reddit, synthesize findings

  into actionable docs that can be handed to other clients (Comms, ClipBot).

  Comms Client location (to copy from): C:\Users\worra\OneDrive\Desktop\comms

  ## What to Copy from Comms Client

  Read these files from C:\Users\worra\OneDrive\Desktop\comms and adapt
  (rename comms вҶ’ research, adjust types and colors):

  - CLI entry: comms/src/cli/index.ts вҶ’ research/src/cli/index.ts
  - Config loader: comms/src/config/loader.ts вҶ’ research/src/config/loader.ts
  - Logger: comms/src/utils/logger.ts вҶ’ research/src/utils/logger.ts
  - Retry: comms/src/utils/retry.ts вҶ’ research/src/utils/retry.ts
  - AI Elements: comms/ui/src/components/ai-elements/* вҶ’ 
  research/ui/src/components/ai-elements/*
  - Sidebar pattern: comms/ui/src/components/layout/* вҶ’ adapt for research nav
  - Contexts: comms/ui/src/contexts/* вҶ’ copy and adapt
  - globals.css: comms/ui/src/app/globals.css вҶ’ copy, change accent color to
  violet (#8B5CF6)
  - Chat API route pattern: comms/ui/src/app/api/chat/route.ts вҶ’ same
  streamText() pattern
  - Store pattern: comms/ui/src/lib/stores/* вҶ’ same read/write JSON file pattern
  - Tool pattern: comms/ui/src/lib/ai/tools/* вҶ’ same tool() + Zod + co-located
  execute pattern

  ## Key Decisions

  - Vercel AI SDK v6 (same as Comms) вҖ” streamText(), useChat(), stopWhen:
  stepCountIs(10)
  - Tools split into separate files by domain вҖ” one file per concern
  - Stores split by entity вҖ” one file per data type
  - 3 pages only: Chat, Briefs, Settings (no placeholder pages)
  - Dark theme with violet accent (#8B5CF6) for research, distinct from Comms
  cyan and ClipBot blue
  - Sidebar has 3 items: Chat, Briefs, Settings
  - Perplexity and NotebookLM tools are OPTIONAL вҖ” they work if API keys are
  set,
    gracefully skip if not. The client works without them using just Firecrawl +

    Playwright + Reddit + Claude's own synthesis.

  ## Tools the AI Can Call

  | Tool | File | What It Does | Requires API Key |
  |------|------|-------------|-----------------|
  | scrape_site | tools/scrape.ts | Scrape a URL вҶ’ structured markdown/data via 
  Firecrawl | FIRECRAWL_API_KEY (free tier) |
  | crawl_domain | tools/scrape.ts | Crawl entire domain вҶ’ all pages via
  Firecrawl | FIRECRAWL_API_KEY (free tier) |
  | browse_page | tools/browse.ts | Navigate to URL, interact with page via 
  Playwright | None (free) |
  | screenshot_page | tools/browse.ts | Screenshot a page via Playwright | None
  (free) |
  | extract_data | tools/browse.ts | Extract structured data from page via 
  Playwright | None (free) |
  | search_reddit | tools/reddit.ts | Search Reddit posts/comments by query +
  subreddit | None (free, public API) |
  | query_notebook | tools/notebook.ts | Ask a question to a NotebookLM notebook
   | Google auth (free) |
  | create_notebook | tools/notebook.ts | Create a new NotebookLM notebook |
  Google auth (free) |
  | add_source | tools/notebook.ts | Add a URL/doc/text as source to a notebook 
  | Google auth (free) |
  | deep_research | tools/perplexity.ts | Deep AI-powered research via
  Perplexity Sonar Pro | PERPLEXITY_API_KEY (optional) |
  | reason | tools/perplexity.ts | Complex reasoning via Perplexity Reasoning
  Pro | PERPLEXITY_API_KEY (optional) |
  | generate_brief | tools/briefs.ts | AI compiles research findings into 
  structured brief | None (uses Claude) |
  | get_briefs | tools/briefs.ts | List all saved briefs | None |
  | get_brief | tools/briefs.ts | Get a specific brief by ID | None |
  | get_settings | tools/settings.ts | View current config | None |

  ## Implementation Steps

  ### Step 1: Root CLI scaffold
  - Create research/ directory structure + package.json + tsconfig.json
  - Copy+adapt from Comms: CLI entry, config loader, logger, retry
  - Types: config.ts, brief.ts, scrape.ts, activity.ts (all with Zod)
  - npm install (commander, chalk, dotenv, zod, tsx)
  - Verify: npx tsx src/cli/index.ts shows banner + help

  ### Step 2: UI scaffold
  - Create research/ui/ with Next.js setup
  - package.json deps: ai, @ai-sdk/anthropic, @ai-sdk/react, next, react,
    motion, lucide-react, streamdown, use-stick-to-bottom, zod
  - next.config.ts, postcss.config.mjs, tsconfig
  - globals.css with dark theme (violet accent #8B5CF6)
  - npx shadcn@latest init + add button, badge, tooltip, collapsible
  - Verify: npm run dev starts on localhost:3000

  ### Step 3: Stores
  - Create lib/stores/briefs.ts вҖ” CRUD for briefs.json
  - Create lib/stores/sources.ts вҖ” CRUD for sources.json (tracks all scraped
  URLs)
  - Create lib/stores/settings.ts вҖ” CRUD for settings.json
  - Create lib/stores/activity.ts вҖ” append-only activity log
  - Each store follows Comms pattern: readFile вҶ’ JSON.parse, writeFile вҶ’
  JSON.stringify

  ### Step 4: AI tools
  - Create lib/ai/tools/scrape.ts вҖ” scrape_site + crawl_domain
    - Uses Firecrawl API (https://api.firecrawl.dev/v1)
    - Saves results to sources store
    - Graceful fallback if no FIRECRAWL_API_KEY (return error message)
  - Create lib/ai/tools/browse.ts вҖ” browse_page + screenshot_page + extract_data
    - Uses Playwright MCP or direct Playwright API
    - Saves results to sources store
  - Create lib/ai/tools/reddit.ts вҖ” search_reddit
    - Uses Reddit public JSON API
  (https://www.reddit.com/r/{subreddit}/search.json)
    - No API key needed вҖ” public endpoint
    - Returns post titles, scores, comment counts, URLs
  - Create lib/ai/tools/notebook.ts вҖ” query_notebook + create_notebook +
  add_source
    - Wraps NotebookLM MCP (https://github.com/PleasePrompto/notebooklm-mcp or 
      https://github.com/jacob-bd/notebooklm-mcp-cli)
    - Graceful fallback if not configured
  - Create lib/ai/tools/perplexity.ts вҖ” deep_research + reason
    - Uses Perplexity API (https://api.perplexity.ai)
    - Graceful fallback if no PERPLEXITY_API_KEY (return "Perplexity not
  configured" message)
  - Create lib/ai/tools/briefs.ts вҖ” generate_brief + get_briefs + get_brief
    - generate_brief: takes topic + sources from store, uses Claude to
  synthesize
      into structured brief with sections: Summary, Key Findings, Sources,
      Recommendations, Action Items
    - Saves brief to briefs store
  - Create lib/ai/tools/settings.ts вҖ” get_settings
  - Create lib/ai/tools/index.ts вҖ” re-export all tools

  ### Step 5: Chat API route + system prompt
  - app/api/chat/route.ts using streamText() вҖ” EXACT same pattern as Comms:
    ```typescript
    import { streamText, stepCountIs } from 'ai';
    import { anthropic } from '@ai-sdk/anthropic';
    import * as tools from '@/lib/ai/tools';
    import { systemPrompt } from '@/lib/ai/system-prompt';

    export async function POST(req: Request) {
      const { messages } = await req.json();
      const result = streamText({
        model: anthropic('claude-sonnet-4-20250514'),
        system: systemPrompt,
        messages,
        tools,
        stopWhen: stepCountIs(10),
      });
      return result.toDataStreamResponse();
    }
  - app/api/briefs/route.ts вҖ” GET (list) + POST (save)
  - app/api/settings/route.ts вҖ” GET + POST
  - system-prompt.ts вҖ” research-specific:
  "You are a research assistant. You help users investigate markets, find
  competitors,
   scrape websites, search Reddit, and compile findings into structured briefs.
   Always cite sources. When you scrape or browse, save results to the sources
  store.
   When asked to compile or summarize, use generate_brief to create a formal
  brief."

  Step 6: Chat UI

  - Copy AI Elements from Comms (conversation.tsx, message.tsx, tool.tsx,
  shimmer.tsx, code-block.tsx)
  - Build chat/prompt-input.tsx, chat/chat-feed.tsx (same as Comms)
  - Build chat/source-card.tsx вҖ” shows scraped URL + excerpt + timestamp
  (renders when scrape/browse tools return results)
  - Main page.tsx with useChat from @ai-sdk/react
    - Hero: "Research" title, "Ask anything. Get briefs." subtitle
    - Chat feed with message/tool rendering
    - Source cards inline when scrape/browse results come back

  Step 7: Layout + briefs page + settings page

  - Sidebar with nav: Chat, Briefs, Settings (3 items only)
  - SidebarContext + ThreadContext providers in layout.tsx
  - /briefs page вҖ” list of saved briefs, click to expand full brief
    - Each brief shows: title, date, topic, source count, summary preview
  - /settings page:
    - API keys: FIRECRAWL_API_KEY, PERPLEXITY_API_KEY
    - NotebookLM configuration
    - Default research preferences

  Verification

  1. cd research && npm install && npx tsx src/cli/index.ts вҶ’ banner + help
  2. cd research/ui && npm install && npm run dev вҶ’ Next.js on localhost:3000
  3. Chat: "search reddit r/cannabis for complaints about dispensary software"
  вҶ’ search_reddit tool runs вҶ’ shows posts with scores
  4. Chat: "scrape the pricing page at https://example.com/pricing"
  вҶ’ scrape_site tool runs вҶ’ shows extracted data + saved to sources
  5. Chat: "compile a brief on everything we've found"
  вҶ’ generate_brief tool runs вҶ’ brief saved вҶ’ shows formatted brief
  6. Navigate to /briefs вҶ’ see saved brief вҶ’ click to expand
  7. Navigate to /settings вҶ’ configure API keys
  8. Sidebar navigation works across all pages

  Theme

  - Dark background (same as Comms)
  - Violet accent: #8B5CF6 (distinct from Comms cyan #06B6D4 and ClipBot blue
  #007AFF)
  - Green for sources/citations: #10B981
  - Same card system, same sidebar, same AI Elements
